and fashion designers follow similar work principles. Clothing and architecture are both occupied with our bodies, they both serve as shelters and are designed around their proportions. They both share history and culture. According to Adedotun Adeyeye, the creative director of menswear brand FRESHBYDOTUN, imagination and creativity are products of Architecture and Fashion, they cross-pollinate. In this self styled editorial, the designer was influenced by his architectural discipline laying emphasis on shapes, forms and proportions. He resembled this to the the creation of buildings themselves, offering form, function and beauty.\\n\\nLook 5 inspiration: geometric shapes and figures made up of lines.\\n\\n\ud83d\udcf8 and fashion designers follow similar work principles. Clothing and architecture are both occupied with our bodies, they both serve as shelters and are designed around their proportions. They both share history and culture. According to Adedotun Adeyeye, the creative director of menswear brand FRESHBYDOTUN, imagination and creativity are products of Architecture and Fashion, they cross-pollinate. In this self styled editorial, the designer was influenced by his architectural discipline laying emphasis on shapes, forms and proportions. and fashion designers follow similar work principles. Clothing and architecture are both occupied with our bodies, they both serve as shelters and are designed around their proportions. They both share history and culture. According to Adedotun Adeyeye, the creative director of menswear brand FRESHBYDOTUN, imagination and creativity are products of Architecture and Fashion, they cross-pollinate. In this self styled editorial, the designer was influenced by his architectural discipline laying emphasis on shapes, forms and proportions.
